activation.\n    $menu.menuAim({\n        activate: activateSubmenu,\n        deactivate: deactivateSubmenu\n    });\n    // jQuery-menu-aim: </meaningful part of the example>\n\n    // jQuery-menu-aim: the following JS is used to show and hide the submenu\n    // contents. Again, this can be done in any number of ways. jQuery-menu-aim\n    // doesn't care how you do this, it just fires the activate and deactivate\n    // events at the right times so you know when to show and hide your submenus.\n    function activateSubmenu(row) {\n        var $row = $(row),\n            submenuId = $row.data(\"submenuId\"),\n            $submenu = $(\"#\" + submenuId),\n            height = $menu.outerHeight(),\n            width = $menu.outerWidth();\n\n        // Show the submenu\n        $submenu.css({\n            display: \"block\",\n            //top: -1,\n            left: width - 3,  // main should overlay submenu\n            //height: height - 4  // padding for main dropdown's arrow\n        });\n\n        // Keep the currently activated row's highlighted look\n        $row.find(\"a\").addClass(\"maintainHover\");\n    }\n\n    function deactivateSubmenu(row) {\n        var $row = $(row),\n            submenuId = $row.data(\"submenuId\"),\n            $submenu = $(\"#\" + submenuId);\n\n        // Hide the submenu and remove the row's highlighted look\n        $submenu.css(\"display\", \"none\");\n        $row.find(\"a\").removeClass(\"maintainHover\");\n    }\n\n    // Bootstrap's dropdown menus immediately close on document click.\n    // Don't let this event close the menu if a submenu is being clicked.\n    // This event propagation control doesn't belong in the menu-aim plugin\n    // itself because the plugin is agnostic to bootstrap.\n    $(\".dropdown-menu li\").click(function(e) {\n        e.stopPropagation();\n    });\n\n    $(document).click(function() {\n        // Simply hide the submenu on any click. Again, this is just a hacked\n        // together menu/submenu structure to show the use of jQuery-menu-aim.\n        $(\".popover\").css(\"display\", \"none\");\n        $(\"a.maintainHover\").removeClass(\"maintainHover\");\n    });\n \n</script>    </div>\n</div>\n\n<noscript>\n  &lt;div class=\"noscript-warning\"&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\"content\"&gt;This site Seed</h2>\n\n\n<h1 style=\"font-size:18px; font-weight:100; text-align:center;\">Welcome to Sustainable Seed Co. - Your Source for Certified Organic Heirloom Seeds</h1>\n\n\n\n<h3 align=\"center\">Since 2008, we've been offering heirloom seeds, garden seeds, and organic heirloom seeds - non-hybrid vegetable, flower, and herb seeds. We are America's best source for  heirloom vegetable seeds, heritage grains and  herb seeds.</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>We wanted to offer heirloom seeds for one reason: they're not only our history, but our security. You can save the seeds of the vegetables, herbs and grains we offer, and with the proper methods, reliably get the same plants for generations to come. We're also a CERTIFIED ORGANIC seed farm - setting us apart from many others who only resell seed. With over 1,800 varieties for you to choose from (over 700 of them bulk seed and 600 of them organic seeds), we're also the web's premiere source for backyard gardeners and farmers alike.  </p>\n\n\n\n\n\n<div class=\"clearfix m0-1\">\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n <div id=\"home-column-wrapper\" style=\"padding-top:20px;\">\n\n\n\n    \t<div class=\"column left\">\n\n\n\n            <h2><b><i>Latest Blog Post</i></b></h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  <h2>\n\n\n\n    <a href=\"http://sustainableseedco.com/blog/a-word-from-our-sponsors/\">\n\n\n\n      A word from our sponsors ;)\n\n\n\n    </a>\n\n\n\n  </h2>\n\n\n\n  Michelle Banks of Northeast Park Preschool in Florida came to our attention one day when she emailed us an utterly adorable picture of two of her students â€“ eating carrots.Â&nbsp; Normally thatâ€™s not so note-worthy, but, well Kyla and Calvin were so darned cute, AND they were eating carrots they planted â€“ from seed! Our seeds are certified organic and are always non-GMO. We offer one of the largest selections of seeds in the county at 1,875 rare heirloom seed varieties and growing.  Sustainable Seed Company has all your favorite vegetable seeds as well as a large collection of specialty varieties such as wheat seeds and other grains, tobacco seeds, herb seeds, flower seeds and cover crops. Sustainable Seed Company also offers bulk seeds for our farming partners.</p>\n\n<p>Sustainable Seed Company  carries many specialty seed mixes including wildflower seeds, herb and salsa packs, mixed pepper seeds, mixed tomato seeds, market garden mix, poultry pack, kids favorites mix, and essential grains. We have several seed bank mixes - or \"gardens in a can\" which are great to use, store or give as gifts. </p>\n\n<p>Whether you are a seasoned master gardener or just starting out, we have all the resources you need for successful growing. Check out our online videos, tips and gardening books. Or, sign up for our monthly newsletter. Be sure to connect with us on <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/SustainableSeed\" target=\"_blank\">Facebook</a> where nearly 60,000 fellow gardeners are actively posting great information every day. Also checkout our Seed Blog, where we give great gardening tips, recipies, and in depth articles to help you become a better grower of your own food. Finally, don't forget our <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/user/sustainableseedco\" target=\"_blank\">YouTube Channel </a>where you can catch great videos on what's going on around here as well as good product videos.</p>\n\n<p>Sustainable Seed Company values food independence and sustainability through green agricultural and business practices. Our mission is to ensure the future of food by saving one of our most precious resources - seeds! Remember...good food comes from good seed.</p>\n\n<p>We have signed the <a href=\"/seed-pledge/seed-pledge.html\" title=\"Safe Seed Pledge\">Safe Seed Pledge</a>, as well as testing where we can any seeds we think might be at risk for GMO contamination. Through sourcing first organic seeds, and then non-organic seeds, we strive to support and expand the organic offerings not only for you our customer, but also to support the farmers who are trying to make a living as Organic Farmers. </p>\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div style=\"float: right !important; width: 48% !important;\">\n\n            <h2><b><i>Company History</i></b></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Sustainable Seed Company's founder, John Fendley, or \"Farmer John\",  got the idea to start a seed company while reading through a book of  known vegetable varieties. He was dismayed to find that  many of the varieties he wanted to grow were  no longer available. John had seen his grandmother feed a family of seven from her garden, and knew that access to good seed is the foundation of food security and a lifeline to cultural heritage. He saw the opportunity to put rare heirloom seeds back into the hands of gardeners and farmers, and from his experience as the owner of a retail nursery, he knew the public was hungry for them.</p>\n\n<p>John founded Sustainable Seed Company in 2008 with Theo Bill, whose experience in marketing and graphic design complemented John’s horticultural knowledge and business savvy.  They chose the name \"Sustainable Seed\" to express how this sensibility runs through every aspect of the company. For example, Sustainable Seed Company sources its seed packaging and shipping materials with the most rigorous, comprehensive and ground-breaking standards in the industry, including Cradle to Cradle, Sustainable Forestry Initiative, and the Program for the Endorsement of Forest Certification. </p>\n\n<p>Our first retail store was in in Monte Rio, CA, and offered 76 varieties that first year.  The business took off, and it wasn’t long before a customer offered us space to farm on her organic vineyard in Forestville, CA.  They began to produce seed on the certified organic winery, with seed stock sourced from the extensive collection of seed bank John had amassed.</p>\n\n<p>In another few years the company was ready to purchase its own farm, and chose the agricultural community of Covelo, CA in Mendocino County, the first county in the U.S. to outlaw the production of genetically engineered crops.  Having its own certified organic farm allowed Sustainable Seed Company to advance its goals of sustainably producing the best varieties of heirloom vegetables for organic growing conditions.  A wind turbine and a large freestanding solar array provided over two thirds of the power to run the company’s operations.  We became a charter member of Partners for Sustainable Pollination, a collaborative effort comprising farmers, growers, beekeepers and scientists working to improve the health of honey bees and support native pollinators.</p>\n\n<p>For several years Sustainable Seed Company operated successfully in the Covelo location and grew so fast that the company saw the need to relocate to a larger area. In 2015 the company moved to the agricultural hub of Chico, CA. It's the perfect location for a growing seed company with a Mediterranean climate that's best for seed production, closer proximity to shipping and distribution centers, and plenty of space to expand the warehouse and farming operations. The new location also offers a retail store that is open to the public.</p>\n\n<p>Our thanks go out to all our customers who have been using Sustainable Seed Company's organic and heirloom seeds over these last several years and we are excited to be growing even more! Stay tuned for more news of our expansion and new varieties of seeds that we'll be adding soon. We are always on the look-out for rare varieties to add to our growing collection so please share your seed story with us online or at our new store.<br>\n\n</p>\n\n\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div
